<section id="aave-documentation" class="Section__Container-sc-pbf9d7-1 fuBEyG"><h1 class="Components__StyledH1-sc-452rcd-11 cKUcLX">Aave Documentation</h1><a href="#aave-documentation" class="Section__DeepLink-sc-pbf9d7-0 cjfsaE"><svg width="13" height="14" viewBox="0 0 13 14" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><path d="M5.39979 3.91466L6.55689 2.75757C6.81014 2.50431 7.1108 2.30342 7.44169 2.16636C7.77258 2.0293 8.12723 1.95876 8.48538 1.95876C8.84354 1.95876 9.19819 2.0293 9.52908 2.16636C9.85997 2.30342 10.1606 2.50431 10.4139 2.75757C10.6671 3.01082 10.868 3.31148 11.0051 3.64237C11.1421 3.97326 11.2127 4.32791 11.2127 4.68606C11.2127 5.04422 11.1421 5.39887 11.0051 5.72976C10.868 6.06065 10.6671 6.36131 10.4139 6.61456L9.25678 7.77166M6.94259 10.0859L5.78549 11.243C5.53224 11.4962 5.23158 11.6971 4.90069 11.8342C4.5698 11.9712 4.21515 12.0418 3.85699 12.0418C3.13367 12.0418 2.43997 11.7544 1.9285 11.2429C1.41703 10.7315 1.12969 10.0378 1.12969 9.31445C1.12969 8.59113 1.41703 7.89743 1.9285 7.38596L3.08559 6.22886" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"></path><path d="M4.62842 8.54297L7.71401 5.45737" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="1.5" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round"></path></svg></a></section>
<p class="Components__StyledParagraph-sc-452rcd-7 grbOYA">Aave is a decentralised non-custodial liquidity protocol where users can participate as suppliers or borrowers. Suppliers provide liquidity to the market while earning interest, and borrowers can access liquidity by providing collateral that exceeds the borrowed amount.</p>
